If your bike needs work take it to Archer Bicycle.<//Text>

<text>Whoah, integrity! Greg worked on my vintage racing bike. The rear gears never shifted smoothly and had been steadily declining. He was able to diagnose the problem immediately and then spent a couple of months tracking down the right part to make the repair--not an easy feat with an obscure bike in times of Covid (when everyone has snatched up spare parts to repair their bike). My gears now shift like butter. Well worth the wait.< /text></record>

<Text>I found Archer after my bike's rear tire spontaneously lost air just two days after I brought it out of my storage, where it had remained dormant for almost a year. Greg was extremely welcoming, and got me set up with a new tube and tire in no time at all. The price was very reasonable and I had a great experience from start to finish. Greg answered all of my questions with enthusiasm, corrected my front brake being a little off, and even gave me a brief lesson in how to spot counterfeit bills after I inquired about one posted to his whiteboard. If you're reading through reviews trying to decide which Oakland bike shop to go to, save yourself some time and just head here!< /Text></record>

< Review>
Craig is incredible.  He will take the time to teach you about anything you ask about if you want to learn.  I asked about reinforced tires and what else other than Gatorskins there was, he pulls out tire pieces that have been cut to about a foot in length and proceeds to show me  the difference of each, performance vs protection of all.  In addition, while his "tune" is more expensive than your typical one at one of the larger chain shops, you get what amounts to everything those stores sell for a lot more in the "full" or "premium" tune.  He also includes a "slush fund" in your tune of 30 dollars that keeps him from having to call you because a 5 dollar part (like brake pads) are needed!

The gallery upstairs had a photog graffiti exhibit, there's a classic pinball in the store, the items he sells are things he personally recommends and his years of experience spills forth in every encounter.  His turnaround time is generally on par or better (barring a sudden influx of work showing up) than most other stores.  The best part?  None of that "bike-bro pretentiousness" you get at other 'hipster cool' shops in the area.<//Review>

< review>
Super great place to hunker for a night on a long drive. I asked to stay (I'm in a pickup) and was welcomed. Security cameras, food, clean bathrooms. The ladies at night were keen and the next morning the two "young" fellas were good for a laugh. Spots for 3+ tractors and vans but I parked enough away as to not be at all annoyed by idling diesel engines. 395 is dead quiet at night here. A gem for a safe night with friendly people and inexpensive fuel (compared to Bishop, Lee Vining and Bridgeport). Will become a regular spot.</review>

When I did a quick google search for other programs in the area this school popped up!

When I called this school the receptionist Kristin answered. She was very polite and placed me on a brief hold while the Admissions Department was reached.

I spoke with the Admissions Department for about thirty minutes. I had many questions related to pricing, class schedule, flexibility, Professor background etc. After ending my call I received supplemental documentation to further educate me on the program.

I found myself in Old Town today and I did a walk by Campus. When I am ready to fully commit myself to a program I will be setting up a meeting. Beginning my MFT is a dream of mine and I think I may have found my perfect school. Very professional, and exceptional service.< /Text>

Updated on  06.13.2016:
The next day after I posted my review, the management contacted me and we had a meeting. I was given an opportunity to share my concerns in detail and get explanations on why the policies I disliked have to be in place. I was also told that my suggestions and complaints will be taken into consideration in the future. Although this does not fix my past experiences, I believe this was a big step forward and that's why I'm increasing my rating to 4 stars.

Previous review:
I used to be a student at this school.

I give 5 stars to almost all the teachers, the location and reasonable tuition fees. However, I give 1 star to most policies, staff members and their customer service skills.

Their registration system is very confusing and complicated. If you need any type of assistance, it's very difficult to reach the right person and get your questions answered. It takes many hours or days to get simple things resolved. They do not value the students' time at all and there have been numerous occasions when I felt treated like garbage.

The only person who is truly committed to helping students is Elvis.

Please keep in mind that laptops are not allowed in classrooms. Laptops can be such a great learning tool in the 21st century...

If you read manager's responses to some of the negative reviews, you'll see something like "please contact us" but there is no specific phone number, no email address and no name. Good luck trying to call them!

Unless you need a student visa, I recommend this school to people who like to waste their time.</review>

Very charming little eatery...my hubby got the carnitas torta and it was delicious! I got the chicken wrap and it was very fresh, healthy, and yummy. My son had the nutella waffle and loved it! Our little one opted for the mint chip milkshake, and it is now her favorite milkshake she's tasted! Everyone is so sweet there and we are excited to try more off their menu when we go again!
*Update to my first review: I now go here almost once a week, if not more. Honestly, I am obsessed! The chicken wrap is my go-to lunch or even dinner, when I am in a hurry and need something quick and healthy. I love the mango agua fresca!! It is delicious and refreshing! My son, along with all of my friends that I have brought here, are diggin' the carnitas torta. It is seriously the best torta I or any of them have had! It is toasted perfectly and the carnitas is so tasty. I looked around more, now that I have visited pretty regularly, and the decor is so cute! A lot of time and love went into this place and you can tell that the owner(s) really have a passion for what they do. Lexi and Alejandra are just two of the girls that I know who work here, and they are both Sweethearts and always are smiling and making sure my order is perfect. Thank you, girls! My family and I will continue to support Dulce Sabor for as long as they're around!</text>

I have ate at the Brownsville Station on several occasions. I think the prices are too high for the product. Even with it being a little pricey, I am partial to the artichoke dip that they  serve with veggies and pita bread, which I usually subsitute with a regular toasted roll instead of the pita bread. Its a clean establishment with clean restrooms. In addition they have free wi-fi service along  with cell service. The waiters are pleasant and very courteous. Service is quick and,efficient.<//review>

< review>
I have eaten at nearly every restraunt in oroville and surrounding areas. Over all the places to eat. This is the place I choose to go, and probally allways will. Service couldnt be better, and the same goes for the food. I'm from San Diego were I have experienced a flurry of foods, and I havent had anything like it. Every menu item is bomb. No matter what you get its fresher then fresh. Sometimes I even eat there twice in one day. I dont know what my life would be with it. Worth the drive, although for me its the same distance into town as it is to the station, although I could see myself driving a couple hours to eat here. I allways eat myself to the point of no more, and the bill is allways cheaper then any other restraunt I would go to achieve this. its crazy how much better real food is then all the proccessed stuff these restraunts pump out. Recomended to everyone everywhere. Max stars. Again bomb.< /review>

<Time>1610217895334</Time><Rate>1</Rate>< review>
Ok! I went to this Trader Joe's for the first time. I was in my nursing apparel and had my badge in hand. I simply wanted to stop by and grab a few items after working a long depressing shift. I presented my badge to the gentleman at the door and he tells me that they are no longer allowing essential workers to enter the store and we are to wait as well. Now I normally shop at the Trader Joe's in Fremont but I relocated to Oakland. Now Healthcare workers don't ask for much and I literally ook that as a Slap in the face. I know that ever RN and physician is incredibly pressed for time because we are all working extremely long, exhausting, and chaotic hours. Now you mean to tell me when we get off we have to stand in line 20 - 30 min. before we can go into a store to make some much needed grocery. I declare this was the 1st and last time that I will ever shop at this Trader Joe's. If I was not so tired and depressed about all the patients that I see dying from CVD everyday, I would have left this store without shopping at all. Plus I just wanted to grab a few things to take to work so that I could have something to eat. This World Truly Have Issues especially when you take a simple gesture and discard during such chaotic times!!!< /review>

They also offer samples everyday of one or more of their products, which can be a helpful way to find something new you'll like that you couldn't afford to take a chance on buying. < Review>
OMG, this is my local Trader Joe's, which I visit on average five times a week, and somehow I've never reviewed it? How's that possible? Argh!

Trader Joe's store #109 is located in the middle of the South Shore Shopping Center. There's hundreds of parking spots immediately out front. Conveniently located near the corner of Park Street and Otis Drive, this is the to-go spot for dozens of staples, some keto-friendly foods (including grilled artichoke hearts, cheeses, eggs, hamburger, pork tenderloin, turkey breast, and sopressata salami), and the many TJ-specific offerings (including truffle p√¢te, many really good coffee beans, and seasonal surprises like unsweetened bakers chocolate, cakes and cookies, and mystery bags).

The non-food items, like greeting cards, plants and flowers, and a wide selection of beer, wine, and hard liquors round out any shopping trip.

The staff are absolutely wonderful, know their stock and where they may be found, and are always ready to help you find a TJ treasure. I'm very proud of my local store and hope you come on over to share in the joy.</Review>

<Time>1494014739732<//Time><Rate>4<//Rate><text>Our go-to store. We come here weekly, because they have a good selection of veggies, fruits, meats, cheeses, snacks, beers and wines. Not to mention the staff is really friendly and the store is well kept (compared to Safeway next door where things are all over the place).

It's not pricey and it's convenient since you have a big parking place and many other stores around (in case you can't get everything here). Sometimes they don't have certain things cause they are changing the labels or getting in something new from someone else, but if you ask they might find something in the back or just tell you the date when they're getting it back on their shelves.

The only downside is that perishable things tend to go bad before their expiration date (salads and fruit I'm looking at you) and we do put them in the fridge and take all the necessary precautions.

The lines are not too long because the staff makes sure there's a sufficient number of check-outs open (again compared to Safeway where you have two registers and 20 people). But if you want to avoid the place being too crowded come in right after they open.

I don't care much for the samples they have, but I was told they are also good.

Would highly recommend you to come here instead of going into Safeway next door.</text><pics>None</pics>< Resp>
